msg:I brought an elderly person here to stay for a week. I can give you a detailed review:

🚗 Transportation: It is close to Lianhua Road Subway Station and has convenient transportation.

🍃Environment: This time I booked a garden view room, facing the small park by the river, with an elevated road not far away. I have stayed in a room with a normal view before, facing a large residential building. It doesn't feel like there's much difference, and the surrounding area isn't originally a scenic spot.

Room: There are transom windows for good ventilation. The air conditioner seems to only be able to adjust the air volume, but not the temperature. If you are not used to sleeping on thick pillows, you can ask room service for a latex pillow, but I personally feel that latex pillows are not very comfortable. It is commendable that the four-piece bed set is very clean! Very comfortable to sleep on.

🧹Hygiene: The hygiene in the room is pretty good, and the cleaning service staff are very friendly. During the Chris**as rush, there may be too many people, and some small details are not done well: ①For example, there are still hairs under the luggage rack where the shoes are placed. ②The carpet is not properly vacuumed. During non-peak periods, the hygiene is pretty good, and customers' needs are responded to in a timely manner. Thank you to the cleaning and subsequent staff.

🔔Service: The hotel staff are very friendly, especially ① the tall concierge intern who helps with luggage in the lobby ② and the concierge at the door who helps with the door and luggage, they are all proactive in helping ③ Vivian who handles check-out at the front desk is also very helpful major. I just don’t know why, but they asked me to deposit a deposit of 5,000 yuan on a daily basis when I checked in. This is not understandable and I feel it is unnecessary.

Hotel breakfast: There are wontons, noodles, Chinese stir-fries, Western salads, bread desserts, coffee milk, etc. It is relatively fresh and tastes good, but there are not many varieties.

Jingxiangxuan: The food is generally good, better than other restaurants. But the production is not very stable, and the same dish is cooked in a different way every other day. Cold dishes such as Nanjing salted duck and drunken chicken tasted unsatisfactory. The portions of some hot dishes are inconsistent, but the taste of the hot dishes is generally okay. Maybe it’s mainly for the private room service. Ordering dishes for individual customers is a bit risky, so be careful about lightning protection, or try to order the same dishes as in the private rooms.

Complaints: ① There is really something wrong with the refrigerator in the room. I used a thermometer to measure 22 degrees in the refrigerator. After the refrigerator was taken out of the cabinet, it was still 10 degrees inside. It is really inconvenient to have cold medicines that need to be taken at any time, which is not satisfactory. ②The hotel slippers were very slippery when exposed to water, and I almost slipped. ③The quality of disposable toothbrushes is too poor. The bristles are very hard and will hurt your teeth.

Overall, it was a pleasant vacation, and the hotel hardware and software are worthy of recognition. The decoration is relatively new, the overall service attitude is good, it is very warm to stay in the hotel in winter, and the family is very happy.

早餐品種繁多，西點好吃，也存在補貨不及時，服務單薄情況。
行政酒廊暫時關閉，有點遺憾，提供下午茶套餐，以及延時退房。
泳池開到晚上九點半，人比較少。
如果能再多一些親子設施和活動，應該會提升更多些人氣吧。

msg:去年來過一次，今年屬於二刷的酒店，本身很新，入住人不多，房間寬敞，有浴缸。泳池全開，不足10個人在遊。早餐餐廳不大，但是菜品很齊全，中式西式都有，大清早能有鮮榨果汁的餐廳不是哪裡都有的。咖啡機不排隊，生滾廣式粥、桃膠和豆花很驚喜。
遇到的前台，餐廳服務員，打掃阿姨都很客氣，延遲退房，行李寄存，小童物品添加都很給力，我糾結了下要不要完整點評，這家酒店要是熱門起來就少了很多體驗感了。
酒店緊挨着中庚漫遊城，南方商城，蓮花，很多餐飲和遛娃選擇，入住第一天在漫遊城的蹦床樂園遛娃+晚餐了。
錦江樂園1.5km，航宇科普中心1km，這距離打車或者步行都ok的，入住第二天去了錦江樂園，第三天去了航宇中心，這酒店還不夠親子？真的是很好住很好玩的一家五星酒店了！

name:c‍h‍e‍r‍r‍y
info:Deluxe Double Room
info:Stayed in September 2022
info:Family
info:9 Reviews
rating:4.2
posted:Posted September 19, 2022
msg:非常喜歡的酒店，前台的小姐姐很好，升級了房間，對於入住、早餐直接説到位，不需要客人一一詢問。
客房服務送洗漱用品速度也很快，也很禮貌，但是遙控板上有灰噢
泳池邊有躺椅，工作人員會來換毛巾，方便使用，也有教練教小孩子游泳，但是都擁在下到泳池的樓梯處，是否可以請有教練的到泳池另一邊呢？
早餐雖然品種不是特別多，但是該有的都有，而且有用心做，非常喜歡，蛋餅包油條，其實蛋餅很好吃，包油條有點幹了，可以分開，客人自己選擇包或者不包，加點甜麪醬
離店時蔡先生服務也很好，出門上車時，門僮也有幫忙拉車門，總體服務是很好的。酒店對面就是核酸點，也很方便。

msg:先説好的：房間房價，地理位子都可以的，吃東西方便，裝修現代程度也ok，早餐也不錯，關機馬路對面還有個免費小童樂園，免費停車，國慶期間還沒有漲價，作為國產品牌可圈可點。不過我來講點注意事項：1⃣️每個房間靠窗都有個被一塊小木窗蓋住的通風口，風大的時候窗會發出嗚嗚嗚低頻，甚至被吹開……2⃣️浴缸很臟，我自己沖洗了三遍，水才沒有漂着油花。3⃣️進出隔壁mall的二樓小門沒有安檢，隨意進出不安全。4⃣️所有房間送mini吧和延遲退房，所以不要被攜程的推薦房型説明給騙了。5⃣️泳池水還可以就是水温偏冷，30多度的天還是覺得冷，而且開着通向外面的大玻璃門，小孩子也説冷。
